Error Detection</h4>\n                    <strong>Product:</strong> Ninja\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Real-time monitoring detects error (99.7% detection rate)\n                    <br><strong>Time:</strong> < 1 second\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>2. Error Analysis</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Ninja, Copilot, AI Platform\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> AI analyzes error context, root cause, and impact\n                    <br><strong>Time:</strong> 2-5 seconds\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>3. Solution Generation</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Ninja, Copilot\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Generate fix code or configuration change\n                    <br><strong>Time:</strong> 5-10 seconds\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>4. Automated Fix</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Ninja, DevOps\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Apply fix automatically (94.3% success rate)\n                    <br><strong>Time:</strong> 10-30 seconds\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>5. Verification</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Ninja, Enterprise\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Verify fix resolved the issue\n                    <br><strong>Time:</strong> 5-10 seconds\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>6. Documentation</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Ninja, Ledger, Core\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Log incident with blockchain audit trail\n                    <br><strong>Time:</strong> 2-5 seconds\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>7. Notification</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Notify, Copilot\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Notify admins of incident and resolution\n                    <br><strong>Time:</strong> 1-2 seconds\n                </div>\n\n                <div style="text-align: center; margin-top: 20px; padding: 20px; background: white; border-radius: 10px;">\n                    <strong style="font-size: 1.3em; color: #28a745;">Total Time: 25-65 seconds from error to resolution</strong>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class="workflow-section" style="margin-top: 30px;">\n                <h3>Healthcare Workflow (HL7+)</h3>\n                \n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>1. HL7 Message Received</h4>\n                    <strong>Product:</strong> HL7+\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Receive HL7 v2.x or FHIR message from EHR/EMR\n                    <br><strong>Security:</strong> HIPAA-compliant encryption (AES-256)\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>2. Message Validation</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> HL7+, Compliance, Shield\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Validate message format, check for errors, verify security\n                    <br><strong>Output:</strong> Valid message or error report\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>3. Data Transformation</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> HL7+, DataFlow\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Transform HL7 to internal format, extract patient data\n                    <br><strong>Output:</strong> Structured patient data\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>4. Data Storage</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> HL7+, Supreme, Data Platform, Vault\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Store in EHR with encryption and access controls\n                    <br><strong>Security:</strong> HIPAA-compliant storage with audit trails\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>5. Clinical Workflow</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Supreme, Workflow, Analytics\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Trigger clinical workflows (appointments, prescriptions, labs)\n                    <br><strong>Output:</strong> Automated clinical processes\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>6. Self-Healing</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> HL7+, Ninja\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Detect and fix HL7 message errors automatically\n                    <br><strong>Output:</strong> Zero-touch incident response\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>7. Compliance & Audit</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Compliance, Ledger, HL7+\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Log all activities with blockchain audit trail\n                    <br><strong>Output:</strong> HIPAA-compliant audit reports\n                </div>\n\n                <div class="workflow-step">\n                    <h4>8. Notification</h4>\n                    <strong>Products:</strong> Notify, Supreme\n                    <br><strong>Action:</strong> Notify healthcare providers of critical events\n                    <br><strong>Output:</strong> Real-time alerts to clinical staff\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Architecture Diagram -->\n        <div class="section">\n datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import Optional\nfrom jose import JWTError, jwt\nfrom passlib.context import CryptContext\nfrom fastapi import Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordBearer\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nimport os\n\n# Security configuration\nSECRET_KEY = os.getenv("SECRET_KEY", "your-secret-key-change-in-production")\nALGORITHM = "HS256"\nACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES = 30\n\n# Password hashing\npwd_context = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")\n\n# OAuth2 scheme\noauth2_scheme = OAuth2PasswordBearer(tokenUrl="api/auth/login")\n\ndef verify_password(plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:\n    """Verify a password against a hash"""\n    return pwd_context.verify(plain_password, hashed_password)\n\ndef get_password_hash(password: str) -> str:\n    """Hash a password"""\n    return pwd_context.hash(password)\n\ndef create_access_token(data: dict, expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:\n    """Create a JWT access token"""\n    to_encode = data.copy()\n    if expires_delta:\n        expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta\n    else:\n        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)\n    \n    to_encode.update({"exp": expire})\n    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, SECRET_KEY, algorithm=ALGORITHM)\n    return encoded_jwt\n\ndef decode_access_token(token: str) -> dict:\n    """Decode a JWT access token"""\n    try:\n        payload = jwt.decode(token, SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[ALGORITHM])\n        return payload\n    except JWTError:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Could not validate credentials",\n            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n        )\n\nasync def get_current_user(token: str = Depends(oauth2_scheme)):\n    """Get the current authenticated user"""\n    credentials_exception = HTTPException(\n        status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n        detail="Could not validate credentials",\n        headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n    )\n    \n    try:\n        payload = decode_access_token(token)\n        user_id: str = payload.get("sub")\n        if user_id is None:\n            raise credentials_exception\n        return {"user_id": user_id, "email": payload.get("email")}\n    except JWTError:\n        raise credentials_exception\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Check if user already exists\n    existing_user = db.query(User).filter(User.email == user_data.email).first()\n    if existing_user:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n            detail="Email already registered"\n        )\n    \n    # Create new user\n    hashed_password = get_password_hash(user_data.password)\n    new_user = User(\n        email=user_data.email,\n        hashed_password=hashed_password,\n        first_name=user_data.first_name,\n        last_name=user_data.last_name,\n        role=user_data.role,\n        phone=user_data.phone,\n        bar_number=user_data.bar_number\n    )\n    \n    db.add(new_user)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_user)\n    \n    # Create access token\n    access_token_expires = timedelta(minutes=ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)\n    access_token = create_access_token(\n        data={"sub": str(new_user.id), "email": new_user.email},\n        expires_delta=access_token_expires\n    )\n    \n    return {\n        "access_token": access_token,\n        "token_type": "bearer",\n        "user": new_user\n    }\n\n@router.post("/login", response_model=Token)\nasync def login(\n    form_data: OAuth2PasswordRequestForm = Depends(),\n    db: Session = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """Login with email and password"""\n    \n    # Find user by email\n    user = db.query(User).filter(User.email == form_data.username).first()\n    \n    if not user or not verify_password(form_data.password, user.hashed_password):\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,\n            detail="Incorrect email or password",\n            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},\n        )\n    \n    if not user.is_active:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n            detail="Inactive user"\n        )\n    \n    # Create access token\n    access_token_expires = timedelta(minutes=ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)\n    access_token = create_access_token(\n        data={"sub": str(user.id), "email": user.email},\n        expires_delta=access_token_expires\n    )\n    \n    return {\n        "access_token": access_token,\n        "token_type": "bearer",\n        "user": user\n    }\n\n@router.post("/logout")\nasync def logout():\n    """Logout (client-side token removal)"""\n    return {"message": "Successfully logged out"}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}
